[30;1m74 | [0m[35m### General Tradeoffs[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m1. This approach works well when either the initial blockwise reduction is effective, or if the[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35m   reduction at the first combine step is effective. Here "effective" means we have multiple members[0m
[30;1m78 | [0m[35m   group in a block so the blockwise application of groupby-reduce actually reduces values and relea[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35m1. One downside is that the final result will only have one chunk along the new group axis.[0m
[30;1m80 | [0m[35m1. We have two choices for how to construct the intermediate arrays. See below.[0m

[30;1m68 | [0m[35mThe GroupBy reduction is first applied blockwise. Those intermediate results are[0m

[30;1m71 | [0m[35mtill all group results are in one block. At that point the result is[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35m"finalized" and returned to the user.[0m
